	        LEFT JOIN erp_red_alhi_test.trans_jbooks b ON b.trans_id = a.trans_id
	        LEFT JOIN trans_jbooks c ON c.jbooks_id = b.acct_jbooks_id
	        GROUP BY c.trans_id
